     1→# OhMyDoc — QA Regression Suite
     2→
     3→Playwright end-to-end tests for [OhMyDoc](https://ohmydoc.vercel.app), an AI-powered document formatter.
     4→
     5→## What's tested
     6→
     7→| Group | Scenarios |
     8→|-------|-----------|
     9→| **1. Basic Load** | Page title, textarea visible, Format button disabled when empty, placeholder text, no console errors |
    10→| **2. Happy Path — Resume** | Full resume formatting flow, loading state, preview, no raw XML tags |
    11→| **3. Happy Path — Cover Letter** | Cover letter formatting, content verification |
    12→| **4. Mutation Warning** | DOM inspection for divergence/mutation warning elements |
    13→| **5. PDF Export** | Export button disabled before formatting, enabled after, `window.print()` triggered |
    14→| **6. Validation** | Empty and short input keep Format button disabled |
    15→| **7. Skeleton Loading** | Shimmer appears during load, disappears on completion |
    16→| **8. Sample Content** | Sample content availability (button or placeholder), formatting of sample-like content |
    17→
    18→**Total: 15 tests** across 8 feature areas.
    19→
    20→## Requirements
    21→
    22→- Node.js 18+
    23→- Chromium (installed automatically by Playwright)
    24→
    25→## Setup
    26→
    27→```bash
    28→npm install
    29→npx playwright install chromium
    30→```
    31→
    32→## Running tests
    33→
    34→```bash
    35→# Run all tests
    36→npm test
    37→
    38→# Run with visible browser
    39→npx playwright test --headed
    40→
    41→# Run a specific test group
    42→npx playwright test --grep "8"
    43→
    44→# Open HTML report after a run
    45→npm run test:report
    46→```
    47→
    48→## Configuration
    49→
    50→Tests run against `https://ohmydoc.vercel.app` by default.
    51→
    52→Override with the `BASE_URL` environment variable:
    53→
    54→```bash
    55→BASE_URL=https://staging.ohmydoc.vercel.app npx playwright test
    56→```
    57→
    58→Or create a `.env` file:
    59→
    60→```
    61→BASE_URL=https://ohmydoc.vercel.app
    62→```
    63→
    64→## CI notes
    65→
    66→- Tests run serially (1 worker) — the AI formatting API must not be rate-limited by parallel calls
    67→- AI-dependent tests use a 90s timeout with fast-fail on API errors
    68→- `test.slow()` is set on tests that involve AI calls (expected ~10–20s each)
    69→- Screenshots are saved on failure under `test-results/`
    70→
    71→## Known observations
    72→
    73→- **No "Load Sample" button**: Sample content is shown as textarea placeholder text only. Tests 8a/8b/8c adapt accordingly; a dedicated "Try Sample" button would improve first-visit UX.
    74→- **Mutation warning**: A divergence banner appears after formatting (observed in test 4) — this is expected behavior when AI rewrites content.
    75→

    67→// ─── Helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    68→
    69→async function getTextarea(page: Page) {
    70→  return page.locator('textarea');
    71→}
    72→
    73→/**
    74→ * Reliably fill a textarea and wait for Vue's reactive model to update.
    75→ * Uses click + fill + value verification to avoid intermittent fill() issues.
    76→ */
    77→async function fillTextarea(page: Page, text: string): Promise<void> {
    78→  const textarea = page.locator('textarea');
    79→  await textarea.click();
    80→  await textarea.fill(text);
    81→  // Wait for Vue reactivity to process the input event
    82→  await page.waitForTimeout(300);
    83→  // Verify the value was actually set
    84→  const value = await textarea.inputValue();
    85→  if (value.length < 10 && text.length > 10) {
    86→    // Retry once if fill didn't work
    87→    await textarea.click();
    88→    await textarea.fill(text);
    89→    await page.waitForTimeout(500);
    90→  }
    91→}
    92→
    93→async function getFormatButton(page: Page) {
    94→  return page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i });
    95→}
    96→
    97→/**
    98→ * Wait for AI formatting to complete OR for an error state to appear.
    99→ * Returns 'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'.
   100→ * Uses a short-circuit: if error text appears within 15s we don't wait 90s.
   101→ * @param successText Optional text to look for in the preview to confirm success.
   102→ *                    Defaults to 'Alex Rivera'. Pass null to use generic detection.
   103→ */
   104→async function waitForFormattingOutcome(
   105→  page: Page,
   106→  successText: string | null = 'Alex Rivera'
   107→): Promise<'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'> {
   108→  const deadline = Date.now() + 90_000;
   109→  const errorPhrases = [
   110→    'api key is not configured',
   111→    'api key not configured',
   112→    'not configured',
   113→    'try again',
   114→    'error',
   115→    'failed',
   116→  ];
   117→
   118→  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
   119→    // Check for success
   120→    if (successText) {
   121→      const textVisible = await page.getByText(successText, { exact: false }).isVisible().catch(() => false);
   122→      if (textVisible) return 'success';
   123→    } else {
   124→      // Generic check: placeholder gone + Format button back to idle state
   125→      const placeholderGone = !(await page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.').isVisible().catch(() => true));
   126→      const btnIdle = await page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i }).isVisible().catch(() => false);
   127→      if (placeholderGone && btnIdle) return 'success';
   128→    }
   129→
   130→    // Check for API error fast
   131→    const bodyText = (await page.locator('body').innerText().catch(() => '')).toLowerCase();
   132→    if (errorPhrases.some(phrase => bodyText.includes(phrase))) {
   133→      return 'api_error';
   134→    }
   135→
   136→    await page.waitForTimeout(1000);
   137→  }
   138→  return 'timeout';
   139→}

   268→test('4. Mutation/divergence warning element exists in DOM', async ({ page }) => {

   270→  await page.goto(BASE_URL);
   271→
   272→  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);
   273→  await (await getFormatButton(page)).click();
   274→
   275→  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);
   276→

   280→      throw new Error(
   281→        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: Cannot test divergence warning — API key not configured.'
   282→      );
   283→    }
   284→  }
   285→
   286→  if (outcome !== 'success') {
   287→    throw new Error(`Formatting did not complete successfully (outcome: ${outcome})`);
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  // Check for warning/alert elements in DOM (may be hidden)
   291→  const warningSelectors = [
   292→    '[class*="warning"]',
   293→    '[class*="diverge"]',
   294→    '[class*="mutation"]',
   295→    '[role="alert"]',
   296→    '[class*="yellow"]',
   297→    '[class*="caution"]',
   298→    '[class*="banner"]',
   299→  ];
   300→
   301→  let warningFound = false;
   302→  for (const selector of warningSelectors) {
   303→    if (await page.locator(selector).count() > 0) {
   304→      warningFound = true;
   305→      break;
   306→    }
   307→  }
   308→  const html = await page.content();
   309→  const hasDivergenceText = /diverge|mutation|content may have been changed|modified/i.test(html);
   310→
   311→  console.log(`Divergence/mutation warning present in DOM: ${warningFound || hasDivergenceText}`);
   312→  // Informational — passes regardless (warning only shows if divergence > 5%)
   313→  expect(true).toBe(true);
   314→});

Pass null to use generic detection.\n */\nasync function waitForFormattingOutcome(\n  page: Page,\n  successText: string | null = 'Alex Rivera'\n): Promise<'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'> {\n  const deadline = Date.now() + 90_000;\n  // Keep phrases specific to real API configuration errors, not generic UI words\n  const errorPhrases = [\n    'api key is not configured',\n    'api key not configured',\n    'openai api key',\n    'not configured',\n  ];\n\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    // Check for success\n    if (successText) {\n      const textVisible = await page.getByText(successText, { exact: false }).isVisible().catch(() => false);\n      if (textVisible) return 'success';\n    } else {\n      // Generic check: placeholder gone + Format button back to idle state\n      const placeholderGone = !(await page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.').isVisible().catch(() => true));\n      const btnIdle = await page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i }).isVisible().catch(() => false);\n      if (placeholderGone && btnIdle) return 'success';\n    }\n\n    // Check for API error fast\n    const bodyText = (await page.locator('body').innerText().catch(() => '')).toLowerCase();\n    if (errorPhrases.some(phrase => bodyText.includes(phrase))) {\n      return 'api_error';\n    }\n\n    await page.waitForTimeout(1000);\n  }\n  return 'timeout';\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 1. Basic Load \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\ntest('1a. Page title is OhMyDoc', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await expect(page).toHaveTitle(/OhMyDoc/i);\n});\n\ntest('1b. Textarea is visible and accepts input', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  await expect(textarea).toBeVisible();\n  await textarea.fill('test input');\n  await expect(textarea).toHaveValue('test input');\n});\n\ntest('1c. Format button is disabled when textarea is empty', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  await expect(textarea).toHaveValue('');\n  const btn = await getFormatButton(page);\n  await expect(btn).toBeDisabled();\n});\n\ntest('1d. Right panel shows placeholder text initially', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await expect(page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.')).toBeVisible();\n});\n\ntest('1e. No critical console errors on load', async ({ page }) => {\n  const errors: string[] = [];\n  page.on('console', msg => {\n    if (msg.type() === 'error') errors.push(msg.text());\n  });\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');\n  const critical = errors.filter(e =>\n    !e.includes('favicon') &&\n    !e.includes('net::ERR') &&\n    !e.includes('ERR_BLOCKED') &&\n    !e.includes('extension')\n  );\n  expect(critical, `Critical console errors: ${critical.join(', ')}`).toHaveLength(0);\n});\n\ntest('1f. Format button enables when sufficient content is entered', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  const btn = await getFormatButton(page);\n\n  // Start with empty \u2014 should be disabled\n  await expect(btn).toBeDisabled();\n\n  // Fill with a meaningful amount of text (well over 50 chars)\n  await textarea.fill(\n    'Jane Smith \u00b7 jane@example.com \u00b7 Toronto, ON\\n\\nSoftware engineer with 5 years of experience in full-stack web development.'\n  );\n  await page.waitForTimeout(300); // allow Vue reactivity\n\n  await expect(btn, 'Format button should be enabled after entering sufficient content').toBeEnabled({ timeout: 3_000 });\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 2. Happy Path \u2014 Resume \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\ntest('2. Happy path \u2014 resume formatting', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);\n\n  const formatBtn = await getFormatButton(page);\n  await expect(formatBtn).toBeEnabled();\n  await formatBtn.click();\n\n  // Button should show loading state\n  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /formatting/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10_000 });\n\n  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);\n\n  // If API key is missing, fail with a clear message\n  if (outcome === 'api_error') {\n    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n    const hasApiKeyError = /api key is not configured|api key not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText);\n    if (hasApiKeyError) {\n      throw new Error(\n        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: \"OpenAI API key is not configured.\" ' +\n        'The Vercel deployment is missing the required AI API key environment variable. ' +\n        'AI formatting cannot function.'\n      );\n    }\n    throw new Error(`AI formatting returned an error. Page text: ${bodyText.substring(0, 300)}`);\n  }\n\n  expect(outcome, 'Formatting timed out after 90s').toBe('success');\n\n  // Name should be visible\n  await expect(page.getByText('Alex Rivera', { exact: false })).toBeVisible();\n\n  // No raw XML tags in visible content\n  const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n  expect(bodyText, 'Raw XML tags found in rendered preview').not.toMatch(/<\\/?[a-z][^>]*>/);\n\n  // Key resume content should be preserved in the formatted output\n  expect(bodyText, 'Employer \"Acme Corp\" should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Acme Corp/i);\n  expect(bodyText, 'Education should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Berkeley|University of California/i);\n\n  // Preview should render HTML markup (headings, lists) \u2014 not just plain text\n  const pageHtml = await page.content();\n  const hasHtmlStructure = /<(h[1-6]|strong|b|ul|ol|li)\\b/i.test(pageHtml);\n  expect(hasHtmlStructure, 'Formatted preview should render HTML structure (headings/lists), not plain text').toBe(true);\n\n  // Button should return to normal\n  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 5_000 });\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 3. function getTextarea(page: Page) {\n  return page.locator('textarea');\n}\n\n/**\n * Reliably fill a textarea and wait for Vue's reactive model to update.\n * Uses click + fill + value verification to avoid intermittent fill() issues.\n */\nasync function fillTextarea(page: Page, text: string): Promise<void> {\n  const textarea = page.locator('textarea');\n  await textarea.click();\n  await textarea.fill(text);\n  // Wait for Vue reactivity to process the input event\n  await page.waitForTimeout(300);\n  // Verify the value was actually set\n  const value = await textarea.inputValue();\n  if (value.length < 10 && text.length > 10) {\n    // Retry once if fill didn't work\n    await textarea.click();\n    await textarea.fill(text);\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500);\n  }\n}\n\nasync function getFormatButton(page: Page) {\n  return page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i });\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns the sample content button/link if the product provides one.\n * OhMyDoc currently shows sample content in the textarea placeholder only;\n * a dedicated button would be the preferred UX pattern.\n */\nasync function getSampleButton(page: Page) {\n  return page.getByRole('button', { name: /sample/i })\n    .or(page.getByRole('link', { name: /sample/i }))\n    .or(page.getByText(/try sample|load sample|use sample|sample resume/i));\n}\n\n/**\n * Wait for AI formatting to complete OR for an error state to appear.\n * Returns 'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'.\n * Uses a short-circuit: if error text appears within 15s we don't wait 90s.\n * @param successText Optional text to look for in the preview to confirm success.\n *                    Defaults to 'Alex Rivera'. Pass null to use generic detection.\n */\nasync function waitForFormattingOutcome(\n  page: Page,\n  successText: string | null = 'Alex Rivera'\n): Promise<'success' | 'api_error' | 'timeout'> {\n  const deadline = Date.now() + 90_000;\n  // Keep phrases specific to real API configuration errors, not generic UI words\n  const errorPhrases = [\n    'api key is not configured',\n    'api key not configured',\n    'openai api key',\n    'not configured',\n  ];\n\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    // Check for success\n    if (successText) {\n      const textVisible = await page.getByText(successText, { exact: false }).isVisible().catch(() => false);\n      if (textVisible) return 'success';\n    } else {\n      // Generic check: placeholder gone + Format button back to idle state\n      const placeholderGone = !(await page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.').isVisible().catch(() => true));\n      const btnIdle = await page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i }).isVisible().catch(() => false);\n      if (placeholderGone && btnIdle) return 'success';\n    }\n\n    // Check for API error fast\n    const bodyText = (await page.locator('body').innerText().catch(() => '')).toLowerCase();\n    if (errorPhrases.some(phrase => bodyText.includes(phrase))) {\n      return 'api_error';\n    }\n\n    await page.waitForTimeout(1000);\n  }\n  return 'timeout';\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 1. Basic Load \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\ntest('1a. Page title is OhMyDoc', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await expect(page).toHaveTitle(/OhMyDoc/i);\n});\n\ntest('1b. Textarea is visible and accepts input', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  await expect(textarea).toBeVisible();\n  await textarea.fill('test input');\n  await expect(textarea).toHaveValue('test input');\n});\n\ntest('1c. Format button is disabled when textarea is empty', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  await expect(textarea).toHaveValue('');\n  const btn = await getFormatButton(page);\n  await expect(btn).toBeDisabled();\n});\n\ntest('1d. Right panel shows placeholder text initially', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await expect(page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.')).toBeVisible();\n});\n\ntest('1e. No critical console errors on load', async ({ page }) => {\n  const errors: string[] = [];\n  page.on('console', msg => {\n    if (msg.type() === 'error') errors.push(msg.text());\n  });\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');\n  const critical = errors.filter(e =>\n    !e.includes('favicon') &&\n    !e.includes('net::ERR') &&\n    !e.includes('ERR_BLOCKED') &&\n    !e.includes('extension')\n  );\n  expect(critical, `Critical console errors: ${critical.join(', ')}`).toHaveLength(0);\n});\n\ntest('1f. Format button enables when sufficient content is entered', async ({ page }) => {\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  const btn = await getFormatButton(page);\n\n  // Start with empty \u2014 should be disabled\n  await expect(btn).toBeDisabled();\n\n  // Fill with a meaningful amount of text (well over 50 chars)\n  await textarea.fill(\n    'Jane Smith \u00b7 jane@example.com \u00b7 Toronto, ON\\n\\nSoftware engineer with 5 years of experience in full-stack web development.'\n  );\n  await page.waitForTimeout(300); // allow Vue reactivity\n\n  await expect(btn, 'Format button should be enabled after entering sufficient content').toBeEnabled({ timeout: 3_000 });\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 2. Happy Path \u2014 Resume \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\ntest('2. Happy path \u2014 resume formatting', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);\n\n  const formatBtn = await getFormatButton(page);\n  await expect(formatBtn).toBeEnabled();\n  await formatBtn.click();\n\n  // Button should show loading state\n  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /formatting/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10_000 });\n\n  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);\n\n  // If API key is missing, fail with a clear message\n  if (outcome === 'api_error') {\n    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n    const hasApiKeyError = /api key is not configured|api key not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText);\n    if (hasApiKeyError) {\n      throw new Error(\n        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: \"OpenAI API key is not configured.\" ' +\n        'The Vercel deployment is missing the required AI API key environment variable. ' +\n        'AI formatting cannot function.'\n      );\n    }\n    throw new Error(`AI formatting returned an error. Page text: ${bodyText.substring(0, 300)}`);\n  }\n\n  expect(outcome, 'Formatting timed out after 90s').toBe('success');\n\n  // Name should be visible\n  await expect(page.getByText('Alex Rivera', { exact: false })).toBeVisible();\n\n  // No raw XML tags in visible content\n  const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n  expect(bodyText, 'Raw XML tags found in rendered preview').not.toMatch(/<\\/?[a-z][^>]*>/);\n\n  // Key resume content should be preserved in the formatted output\n  expect(bodyText, 'Employer \"Acme Corp\" should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Acme Corp/i);\n  expect(bodyText, 'Education should be preserved in formatted output').toMatch(/Berkeley|University of California/i);\n\n  // Preview should render HTML markup (headings, lists) \u2014 not just plain text\n  const pageHtml = await page.content();\n  const hasHtmlStructure = /<(h[1-6]|strong|b|ul|ol|li)\\b/i.test(pageHtml);\n  expect(hasHtmlStructure, 'Formatted preview should render HTML structure (headings/lists), not plain text').toBe(true);\n\n  // Button should return to normal\n  await expect(page.getByRole('button', { name: /format my resume/i })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 5_000 });\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 3. Happy Path \u2014 Cover Letter \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\ntest('3. Happy path \u2014 cover letter formatting', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  await fillTextarea(page, COVER_LETTER_TEXT);\n\n  const formatBtn = await getFormatButton(page);\n  await expect(formatBtn).toBeEnabled();\n  await formatBtn.click();\n\n  // Use generic detection: placeholder gone + Format button back to idle\n  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page, null);\n\n  if (outcome === 'api_error') {\n    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n    const hasApiKeyError = /api key is not configured|api key not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText);\n    if (hasApiKeyError) {\n      throw new Error(\n        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: \"OpenAI API key is not configured.\" ' +\n        'Cover letter formatting cannot function.'\n      );\n    }\n    throw new Error(`AI formatting returned an error. Page text: ${bodyText.substring(0, 300)}`);\n  }\n\n  expect(outcome, 'Cover letter formatting timed out after 90s').toBe('success');\n\n  // Verify the formatted preview is visible (not placeholder) and TechVision appears\n  await expect(page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.')).not.toBeVisible();\n  await expect(page.getByText('TechVision', { exact: false })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10_000 });\n\n  const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n  expect(bodyText, 'Raw XML tags found in rendered preview').not.toMatch(/<\\/?[a-z][^>]*>/);\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 4. Mutation/divergence warning element exists in DOM', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);\n  await (await getFormatButton(page)).click();\n\n  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);\n\n  if (outcome === 'api_error') {\n    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n    if (/api key is not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText)) {\n      throw new Error(\n        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: Cannot test divergence warning \u2014 API key not configured.'\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (outcome !== 'success') {\n    throw new Error(`Formatting did not complete successfully (outcome: ${outcome})`);\n  }\n\n  // Check for warning/alert elements in DOM (may be hidden)\n  const warningSelectors = [\n    '[class*=\"warning\"]',\n    '[class*=\"diverge\"]',\n    '[class*=\"mutation\"]',\n    '[role=\"alert\"]',\n    '[class*=\"yellow\"]',\n    '[class*=\"caution\"]',\n    '[class*=\"banner\"]',\n  ];\n\n  let warningFound = false;\n  for (const selector of warningSelectors) {\n    if (await page.locator(selector).count() > 0) {\n      warningFound = true;\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n  const html = await page.content();\n  const hasDivergenceText = /diverge|mutation|content may have been changed|modified/i.test(html);\n\n  // Informational log \u2014 warning only appears when AI divergence exceeds threshold\n  console.log(`Divergence/mutation elements found in DOM: ${warningFound || hasDivergenceText}`);\n\n  // Real assertion: formatted content is present and not an error state\n  const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n  expect(bodyText, '\"Alex Rivera\" should appear in formatted output').toContain('Alex Rivera');\n  expect(page.getByText('Your formatted document will appear here.')).not.toBeVisible();\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 5. PDF Export button triggers window.print()', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  // Export PDF button should be disabled initially\n  const exportBtn = page.getByRole('button', { name: /export pdf/i });\n  await expect(exportBtn).toBeDisabled();\n\n  // Format a document first\n  await fillTextarea(page, RESUME_TEXT);\n  await (await getFormatButton(page)).click();\n\n  const outcome = await waitForFormattingOutcome(page);\n\n  if (outcome === 'api_error') {\n    const bodyText = await page.locator('body').innerText();\n    if (/api key is not configured|not configured/i.test(bodyText)) {\n      throw new Error(\n        '[BUG] Deployment misconfiguration: Cannot test PDF Export \u2014 API key not configured. ' +\n        'Export PDF button remains disabled because formatting never completes.'\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  expect(outcome, 'Formatting timed out before PDF export test').toBe('success');\n\n  // Export PDF button should now be enabled\n  await expect(exportBtn).toBeEnabled({ timeout: 10_000 });\n\n  // Intercept window.print()\n  let printCalled = false;\n  await page.exposeFunction('__testPrintCalled', () => { printCalled = true; });\n  await page.evaluate(() => {\n    window.print = () => {\n      (window as any).__testPrintCalled();\n    };\n  });\n\n  await exportBtn.click();\n  await page.waitForTimeout(1000);\n  expect(printCalled, 'window.print() was not called when Export PDF was clicked').toBe(true);\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 6.
